\DoxyCodeLine{285 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{286     \textcolor{comment}{// Context creation and access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{287     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Each context create its own ImFontAtlas by default. You may instance one yourself and pass it to CreateContext() to share a font atlas between contexts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{288     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ DLL users: heaps and globals are not shared across DLL boundaries! You will need to call SetCurrentContext() + SetAllocatorFunctions()}}

\DoxyCodeLine{320     \textcolor{comment}{// Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{321     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() = push window to the stack and start appending to it. End() = pop window from the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{322     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Passing 'bool* p\_open != NULL' shows a window-\/closing widget in the upper-\/right corner of the window,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{323     \textcolor{comment}{//   which clicking will set the boolean to false when clicked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{324     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may append multiple times to the same window during the same frame by calling Begin()/End() pairs multiple times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{325     \textcolor{comment}{//   Some information such as 'flags' or 'p\_open' will only be considered by the first call to Begin().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{326     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Begin() return false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{327     \textcolor{comment}{//   anything to the window. Always call a matching End() for each Begin() call, regardless of its return value!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{328     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{329     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{330     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{331     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Note that the bottom of window stack always contains a window called "{}Debug"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{332     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a581e58db0bc930bafa4a5d23093a2b99}{Begin}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a5c4947d4516dd7cfa3505ce3a648a4ef}{name}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a0b8e067ab4f7a818828c8d89e531addc}{ImGuiWindowFlags}} flags = 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{333     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a5479d93794a004c67ceb6d13f37c8254}{End}}();}
\DoxyCodeLine{334 }
\DoxyCodeLine{335     \textcolor{comment}{// Child Windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{336     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use child windows to begin into a self-\/contained independent scrolling/clipping regions within a host window. Child windows can embed their own child.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{337     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For each independent axis of 'size': ==0.0f: use remaining host window size / >0.0f: fixed size / <0.0f: use remaining window size minus abs(size) / Each axis can use a different mode, e.g. ImVec2(0,400).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{338     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ BeginChild() returns false to indicate the window is collapsed or fully clipped, so you may early out and omit submitting anything to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{339     \textcolor{comment}{//   Always call a matching EndChild() for each BeginChild() call, regardless of its return value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{340     \textcolor{comment}{//   [Important: due to legacy reason, this is inconsistent with most other functions such as BeginMenu/EndMenu,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{341     \textcolor{comment}{//    BeginPopup/EndPopup, etc. where the EndXXX call should only be called if the corresponding BeginXXX function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{342     \textcolor{comment}{//    returned true. Begin and BeginChild are the only odd ones out. Will be fixed in a future update.]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{343     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a5db08f552118a1f946e19b5933dce181}{BeginChild}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a3d1e3edfcf61ca2d831883e1afbad89e}{size}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0), \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a04bf50a0ceff267d0040a99e545d74e9}{border}} = \textcolor{keyword}{false}, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a0b8e067ab4f7a818828c8d89e531addc}{ImGuiWindowFlags}} flags = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{433     \textcolor{comment}{// Cursor / Layout}}
\DoxyCodeLine{434     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ By "{}cursor"{} we mean the current output position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{435     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The typical widget behavior is to output themselves at the current cursor position, then move the cursor one line down.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{436     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can call SameLine() between widgets to undo the last carriage return and output at the right of the preceding widget.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{437     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Attention! We currently have inconsistencies between window-\/local and absolute positions we will aim to fix with future API:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{438     \textcolor{comment}{//    Window-\/local coordinates:   SameLine(), GetCursorPos(), SetCursorPos(), GetCursorStartPos(), GetContentRegionMax(), GetWindowContentRegion*(), PushTextWrapPos()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{439     \textcolor{comment}{//    Absolute coordinate:        GetCursorScreenPos(), SetCursorScreenPos(), all ImDrawList:: functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{440     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a191123597a5084d003c8beac7eeb029e}{Separator}}();                                                    \textcolor{comment}{// separator, generally horizontal. inside a menu bar or in horizontal layout mode, this becomes a vertical separator.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{464     \textcolor{comment}{// ID stack/scopes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{465     \textcolor{comment}{// Read the FAQ (docs/FAQ.md or http://dearimgui.org/faq) for more details about how ID are handled in dear imgui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{466     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Those questions are answered and impacted by understanding of the ID stack system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{467     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: Why is my widget not reacting when I click on it?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{468     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have widgets with an empty label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{469     \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ "{}Q: How can I have multiple widgets with the same label?"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{470     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Short version: ID are hashes of the entire ID stack. If you are creating widgets in a loop you most likely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{471     \textcolor{comment}{//   want to push a unique identifier (e.g. object pointer, loop index) to uniquely differentiate them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{472     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also use the "{}Label\#\#foobar"{} syntax within widget label to distinguish them from each others.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{473     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In this header file we use the "{}label"{}/"{}name"{} terminology to denote a string that will be displayed + used as an ID,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{474     \textcolor{comment}{//   whereas "{}str\_id"{} denote a string that is only used as an ID and not normally displayed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{475     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a27a8533605dc5b8cabf161bf7715bbde}{PushID}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{476     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a27a8533605dc5b8cabf161bf7715bbde}{PushID}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_begin, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id\_end);       \textcolor{comment}{// push string into the ID stack (will hash string).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{477     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a27a8533605dc5b8cabf161bf7715bbde}{PushID}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}* ptr\_id);                                     \textcolor{comment}{// push pointer into the ID stack (will hash pointer).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{478     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a27a8533605dc5b8cabf161bf7715bbde}{PushID}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} int\_id);                                             \textcolor{comment}{// push integer into the ID stack (will hash integer).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{525     \textcolor{comment}{// Widgets: Drag Sliders}}
\DoxyCodeLine{526     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ CTRL+Click on any drag box to turn them into an input box. Manually input values aren't clamped by default and can go off-\/bounds. Use ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp to always clamp.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{527     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For all the Float2/Float3/Float4/Int2/Int3/Int4 versions of every functions, note that a 'float v[X]' function argument is the same as 'float* v',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{528     \textcolor{comment}{//   the array syntax is just a way to document the number of elements that are expected to be accessible. You can pass address of your first element out of a contiguous set, e.g. \&myvector.x}}
\DoxyCodeLine{529     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Adjust format string to decorate the value with a prefix, a suffix, or adapt the editing and display precision e.g. "{}\%.3f"{} -\/> 1.234; "{}\%5.2f secs"{} -\/> 01.23 secs; "{}Biscuit: \%.0f"{} -\/> Biscuit: 1; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{530     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Format string may also be set to NULL or use the default format ("{}\%f"{} or "{}\%d"{}).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{531     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Speed are per-\/pixel of mouse movement (v\_speed=0.2f: mouse needs to move by 5 pixels to increase value by 1). For gamepad/keyboard navigation, minimum speed is Max(v\_speed, minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{532     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_min < v\_max to clamp edits to given limits. Note that CTRL+Click manual input can override those limits if ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{533     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use v\_max = FLT\_MAX / INT\_MAX etc to avoid clamping to a maximum, same with v\_min = -\/FLT\_MAX / INT\_MIN to avoid clamping to a minimum.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{534     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use the same sets of flags for DragXXX() and SliderXXX() functions as the features are the same and it makes it easier to swap them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{535     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Legacy: Pre-\/1.78 there are DragXXX() function signatures that takes a final `float power=1.0f' argument instead of the `ImGuiSliderFlags flags=0' argument.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{536     \textcolor{comment}{//   If you get a warning converting a float to ImGuiSliderFlags, read https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/3361}}
\DoxyCodeLine{537     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_aab1b20e7bf98aa7bbdb26f8cd3ad91e6}{DragFloat}}(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}* v, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_speed = 1.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_min = 0.0f, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} v\_max = 0.0f, const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a1e3b09934060e9d373139c3557730d37}{format}} = "{}\%.3f"{}, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a50cc3e3e4beb155e2186f8c1dc057e18}{ImGuiSliderFlags}} flags = 0);     \textcolor{comment}{// If v\_min >= v\_max we have no bound}}

\DoxyCodeLine{551     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ CTRL+Click on any slider to turn them into an input box. Manually input values aren't clamped by default and can go off-\/bounds. Use ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp to always clamp.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{552     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Adjust format string to decorate the value with a prefix, a suffix, or adapt the editing and display precision e.g. "{}\%.3f"{} -\/> 1.234; "{}\%5.2f secs"{} -\/> 01.23 secs; "{}Biscuit: \%.0f"{} -\/> Biscuit: 1; etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{553     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Format string may also be set to NULL or use the default format ("{}\%f"{} or "{}\%d"{}).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{671     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups, Modals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{672     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They block normal mouse hovering detection (and therefore most mouse interactions) behind them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{673     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{674     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Their visibility state (\string~bool) is held internally instead of being held by the programmer as we are used to with regular Begin*() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{675     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ The 3 properties above are related: we need to retain popup visibility state in the library because popups may be closed as any time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{676     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ You can bypass the hovering restriction by using ImGuiHoveredFlags\_AllowWhenBlockedByPopup when calling IsItemHovered() or IsWindowHovered().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{677     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Popup identifiers are relative to the current ID stack, so OpenPopup and BeginPopup generally needs to be at the same level of the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{678     \textcolor{comment}{//    This is sometimes leading to confusing mistakes. May rework this in the future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{679 }
\DoxyCodeLine{680     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: begin/end functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{681     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopup(): query popup state, if open start appending into the window. Call EndPopup() afterwards. ImGuiWindowFlags are forwarded to the window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{682     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ BeginPopupModal(): block every interactions behind the window, cannot be closed by user, add a dimming background, has a title bar.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{683     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a10e213926d8ca212266bc5fbded1e026}{BeginPopup}}(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a0b8e067ab4f7a818828c8d89e531addc}{ImGuiWindowFlags}} flags = 0);                         \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the popup is open, and you can start outputting to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{684     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a6d840f615c198c2342968f733fda11b3}{BeginPopupModal}}(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a5c4947d4516dd7cfa3505ce3a648a4ef}{name}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}* p\_open = NULL, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a0b8e067ab4f7a818828c8d89e531addc}{ImGuiWindowFlags}} flags = 0); \textcolor{comment}{// return true if the modal is open, and you can start outputting to it.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{686 }
\DoxyCodeLine{687     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: open/close functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{688     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ OpenPopup(): set popup state to open. ImGuiPopupFlags are available for opening options.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{689     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ If not modal: they can be closed by clicking anywhere outside them, or by pressing ESCAPE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{690     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup(): use inside the BeginPopup()/EndPopup() scope to close manually.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{691     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ CloseCurrentPopup() is called by default by Selectable()/MenuItem() when activated (FIXME: need some options).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Use ImGuiPopupFlags\_NoOpenOverExistingPopup to avoid opening a popup if there's already one at the same level. This is equivalent to e.g. testing for !IsAnyPopupOpen() prior to OpenPopup().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Use IsWindowAppearing() after BeginPopup() to tell if a window just opened.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{700     \textcolor{comment}{// Popups: open+begin combined functions helpers}}

\DoxyCodeLine{702     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ They are convenient to easily create context menus, hence the name.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{703     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ IMPORTANT: Notice that BeginPopupContextXXX takes ImGuiPopupFlags just like OpenPopup() and unlike BeginPopup(). For full consistency, we may add ImGuiWindowFlags to the BeginPopupContextXXX functions in the future.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{715     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Full-\/featured replacement for old Columns API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See Demo-\/>Tables for demo code. See top of imgui\_tables.cpp for general commentary.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{718     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ See ImGuiTableFlags\_ and ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_ enums for a description of available flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{719     \textcolor{comment}{// The typical call flow is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 1. Call BeginTable(), early out if returning false.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 2. Optionally call TableSetupColumn() to submit column name/flags/defaults.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 3. Optionally call TableSetupScrollFreeze() to request scroll freezing of columns/rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 4. Optionally call TableHeadersRow() to submit a header row. Names are pulled from TableSetupColumn() data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Populate contents:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{725     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ In most situations you can use TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex(N) to start appending into a column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{726     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ If you are using tables as a sort of grid, where every columns is holding the same type of contents,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{727     \textcolor{comment}{//      you may prefer using TableNextColumn() instead of TableNextRow() + TableSetColumnIndex().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{728     \textcolor{comment}{//      TableNextColumn() will automatically wrap-\/around into the next row if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{729     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ IMPORTANT: Comparatively to the old Columns() API, we need to call TableNextColumn() for the first column!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{730     \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Summary of possible call flow:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{731     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{732     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(0) -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableSetColumnIndex(1) -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{733     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow() -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK}}
\DoxyCodeLine{734     \textcolor{comment}{//                          TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{}) -\/> TableNextColumn()      -\/> Text("{}Hello 1"{})  // OK: TableNextColumn() automatically gets to next row!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{735     \textcolor{comment}{//        TableNextRow()                           -\/> Text("{}Hello 0"{})                                               // Not OK! Missing TableSetColumnIndex() or TableNextColumn()! Text will not appear!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{736     \textcolor{comment}{//        -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{737     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ 5. Call EndTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{738     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a04ee4f6866b8e10b98008e7f19d35796}{BeginTable}}(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* str\_id, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ad3032e379f8aba2cb5c31b05cd40858d}{ImGuiTableFlags}} flags = 0, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& outer\_size = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0.0f, 0.0f), \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} inner\_width = 0.0f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{739     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a9c70aaa6464c2e51e6f3342da133ada1}{EndTable}}();                                         \textcolor{comment}{// only call EndTable() if BeginTable() returns true!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{740     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a33511cbfe04b545a1a51b514ab6c208c}{TableNextRow}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_acff5083d4dbfa7a898927046008598c1}{ImGuiTableRowFlags}} row\_flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min\_row\_height = 0.0f); \textcolor{comment}{// append into the first cell of a new row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{741     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_ac9925e8335f55449b1be988829e37ba5}{TableNextColumn}}();                                  \textcolor{comment}{// append into the next column (or first column of next row if currently in last column). Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{742     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_adfbeb33991944035737d413379ae8b1c}{TableSetColumnIndex}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} column\_n);                  \textcolor{comment}{// append into the specified column. Return true when column is visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{743 }
\DoxyCodeLine{744     \textcolor{comment}{// Tables: Headers \& Columns declaration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{745     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupColumn() to specify label, resizing policy, default width/weight, id, various other flags etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{746     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableHeadersRow() to create a header row and automatically submit a TableHeader() for each column.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{747     \textcolor{comment}{//   Headers are required to perform: reordering, sorting, and opening the context menu.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{748     \textcolor{comment}{//   The context menu can also be made available in columns body using ImGuiTableFlags\_ContextMenuInBody.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{749     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You may manually submit headers using TableNextRow() + TableHeader() calls, but this is only useful in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{750     \textcolor{comment}{//   some advanced use cases (e.g. adding custom widgets in header row).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{751     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use TableSetupScrollFreeze() to lock columns/rows so they stay visible when scrolled.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{752     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}          \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_a4ac0fd352082b1aa9a2a5a1dedcf5b89}{TableSetupColumn}}(const \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* label, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_afa2ab8df5653f1cc944f6cbc156bf874}{ImGuiTableColumnFlags}} flags = 0, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} init\_width\_or\_weight = 0.0f, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a1785c9b6f4e16406764a85f32582236f}{ImGuiID}} user\_id = 0);}

\DoxyCodeLine{792     \textcolor{comment}{// Docking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{793     \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA API] Enable with io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_DockingEnable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{794     \textcolor{comment}{// Note: You can use most Docking facilities without calling any API. You DO NOT need to call DockSpace() to use Docking!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{795     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Drag from window title bar or their tab to dock/undock. Hold SHIFT to disable docking/undocking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{796     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Drag from window menu button (upper-\/left button) to undock an entire node (all windows).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{797     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When io.ConfigDockingWithShift == true, you instead need to hold SHIFT to \_enable\_ docking/undocking.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{798     \textcolor{comment}{// About dockspaces:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{799     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use DockSpace() to create an explicit dock node \_within\_ an existing window. See Docking demo for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{800     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Use DockSpaceOverViewport() to create an explicit dock node covering the screen or a specific viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{801     \textcolor{comment}{//   This is often used with ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_PassthruCentralNode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{802     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: Dockspaces need to be submitted \_before\_ any window they can host. Submit it early in your frame!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{803     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: Dockspaces need to be kept alive if hidden, otherwise windows docked into it will be undocked.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{804     \textcolor{comment}{//   e.g. if you have multiple tabs with a dockspace inside each tab: submit the non-\/visible dockspaces with ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_KeepAliveOnly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{805     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a43829975e84e45d1149597467a14bbf5}{IMGUI\_API}} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a1785c9b6f4e16406764a85f32582236f}{ImGuiID}}       \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_im_gui_aacc87878f9d14939bfbbaa2f719e910e}{DockSpace}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a1785c9b6f4e16406764a85f32582236f}{ImGuiID}} \textcolor{keywordtype}{id}, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}\& \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_a3d1e3edfcf61ca2d831883e1afbad89e}{size}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(0, 0), \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ad2fc6cf2d0116e422921e4ffc1077c6f}{ImGuiDockNodeFlags}} flags = 0, const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_window_class}{ImGuiWindowClass}}* window\_class = NULL);}

\DoxyCodeLine{822     \textcolor{comment}{// Drag and Drop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{823     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On source items, call BeginDragDropSource(), if it returns true also call SetDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropSource().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{824     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ On target candidates, call BeginDragDropTarget(), if it returns true also call AcceptDragDropPayload() + EndDragDropTarget().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{825     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you stop calling BeginDragDropSource() the payload is preserved however it won't have a preview tooltip (we currently display a fallback "{}..."{} tooltip, see \#1725)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1079 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for OpenPopup*(), BeginPopupContext*(), IsPopupOpen() functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1080 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To be backward compatible with older API which took an 'int mouse\_button = 1' argument, we need to treat}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1081 \textcolor{comment}{//   small flags values as a mouse button index, so we encode the mouse button in the first few bits of the flags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1082 \textcolor{comment}{//   It is therefore guaranteed to be legal to pass a mouse button index in ImGuiPopupFlags.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1083 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For the same reason, we exceptionally default the ImGuiPopupFlags argument of BeginPopupContextXXX functions to 1 instead of 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1084 \textcolor{comment}{//   IMPORTANT: because the default parameter is 1 (==ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight), if you rely on the default parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1085 \textcolor{comment}{//   and want to another another flag, you need to pass in the ImGuiPopupFlags\_MouseButtonRight flag.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1086 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Multiple buttons currently cannot be combined/or-\/ed in those functions (we could allow it later).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1087 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a555744cd1c43214047697439a08a086e}{ImGuiPopupFlags\_}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1157 \textcolor{comment}{// Flags for ImGui::BeginTable()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important! Sizing policies have complex and subtle side effects, much more so than you would expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159 \textcolor{comment}{//   Read comments/demos carefully + experiment with live demos to get acquainted with them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DEFAULT sizing policies are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1161 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit    if ScrollX is on, or if host window has ImGuiWindowFlags\_AlwaysAutoResize.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1162 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Default to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame if ScrollX is off.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1163 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is off:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1164 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchSame -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthStretch with same weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1165 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Stretch (default), Fixed/Auto.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns (if any) will generally obtain their requested width (unless the table cannot fit them all).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Stretch Columns will share the remaining width according to their respective weight.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1168 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Mixed Fixed/Stretch columns is possible but has various side-\/effects on resizing behaviors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169 \textcolor{comment}{//      The typical use of mixing sizing policies is: any number of LEADING Fixed columns, followed by one or two TRAILING Stretch columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170 \textcolor{comment}{//      (this is because the visible order of columns have subtle but necessary effects on how they react to manual resizing).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1171 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When ScrollX is on:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1172 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Table defaults to ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingFixedFit -\/> all Columns defaults to ImGuiTableColumnFlags\_WidthFixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1173 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Columns sizing policy allowed: Fixed/Auto mostly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1174 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Fixed Columns can be enlarged as needed. Table will show an horizontal scrollbar if needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1175 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ When using auto-\/resizing (non-\/resizable) fixed columns, querying the content width to use item right-\/alignment e.g. SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN) doesn't make sense, would create a feedback loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1176 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ Using Stretch columns OFTEN DOES NOT MAKE SENSE if ScrollX is on, UNLESS you have specified a value for 'inner\_width' in BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1177 \textcolor{comment}{//      If you specify a value for 'inner\_width' then effectively the scrolling space is known and Stretch or mixed Fixed/Stretch columns become meaningful again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1178 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read on documentation at the top of imgui\_tables.cpp for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1179 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457db}{ImGuiTableFlags\_}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1180 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1181     \textcolor{comment}{// Features}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1182     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba2c14d0c1ce69eb2e290a1bc55c391b06}{ImGuiTableFlags\_None}}                       = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{1183     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbaf01e51eba480c57e9ecb0c7ccf57878d}{ImGuiTableFlags\_Resizable}}                  = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable resizing columns.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1184     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba2c2d05129f42cd655c68ff645b2c916e}{ImGuiTableFlags\_Reorderable}}                = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Enable reordering columns in header row (need calling TableSetupColumn() + TableHeadersRow() to display headers)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1284 \textcolor{comment}{// Enum for ImGui::TableSetBgColor()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1285 \textcolor{comment}{// Background colors are rendering in 3 layers:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1286 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 0: draw with RowBg0 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg0 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1287 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 1: draw with RowBg1 color if set, otherwise draw with ColumnBg1 if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1288 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Layer 2: draw with CellBg color if set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1289 \textcolor{comment}{// The purpose of the two row/columns layers is to let you decide if a background color changes should override or blend with the existing color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1290 \textcolor{comment}{// When using ImGuiTableFlags\_RowBg on the table, each row has the RowBg0 color automatically set for odd/even rows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1291 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg0 target, your color will override the existing RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1292 \textcolor{comment}{// If you set the color of RowBg1 or ColumnBg1 target, your color will blend over the RowBg0 color.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1293 \textcolor{keyword}{enum} \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a76dd5d4a9da6570f67c9d45f8d3e16d6}{ImGuiTableBgTarget\_}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1294 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1488     \textcolor{comment}{// Keyboard Modifiers (explicitly submitted by backend via AddKeyEvent() calls)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1489     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is mirroring the data also written to io.KeyCtrl, io.KeyShift, io.KeyAlt, io.KeySuper, in a format allowing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1490     \textcolor{comment}{//   them to be accessed via standard key API, allowing calls such as IsKeyPressed(), IsKeyReleased(), querying duration etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1491     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Code polling every keys (e.g. an interface to detect a key press for input mapping) might want to ignore those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1492     \textcolor{comment}{//   and prefer using the real keys (e.g. ImGuiKey\_LeftCtrl, ImGuiKey\_RightCtrl instead of ImGuiKey\_ModCtrl).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1493     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In theory the value of keyboard modifiers should be roughly equivalent to a logical or of the equivalent left/right keys.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1494     \textcolor{comment}{//   In practice: it's complicated; mods are often provided from different sources. Keyboard layout, IME, sticky keys and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1495     \textcolor{comment}{//   backends tend to interfere and break that equivalence. The safer decision is to relay that ambiguity down to the end-\/user...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1496     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a683cc5d09c63d74035a98ac3b0dec545a84be0e3742547e90ff0de284f14b024d}{ImGuiKey\_ModCtrl}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a683cc5d09c63d74035a98ac3b0dec545af7973f296bb29f339229df21555eae82}{ImGuiKey\_ModShift}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a683cc5d09c63d74035a98ac3b0dec545abf77dca12af0e3acd943d4512d3dcf8e}{ImGuiKey\_ModAlt}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a683cc5d09c63d74035a98ac3b0dec545ad14dd61bca1ff9bfa25627bce9238877}{ImGuiKey\_ModSuper}},}

May be useful on TV/console systems where moving a virtual mouse is awkward. Will update io.MousePos and set io.WantSetMousePos=true. If enabled you MUST honor io.WantSetMousePos requests in your backend, otherwise ImGui will react as if the mouse is jumping around back and forth.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1835 \textcolor{comment}{// ImVector<>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836 \textcolor{comment}{// Lightweight std::vector<>-\/like class to avoid dragging dependencies (also, some implementations of STL with debug enabled are absurdly slow, we bypass it so our code runs fast in debug).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You generally do NOT need to care or use this ever. But we need to make it available in imgui.h because some of our public structures are relying on it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ We use std-\/like naming convention here, which is a little unusual for this codebase.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: clear() frees memory, resize(0) keep the allocated buffer. We use resize(0) a lot to intentionally recycle allocated buffers across frames and amortize our costs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: our implementation does NOT call C++ constructors/destructors, we treat everything as raw data! This is intentional but be extra mindful of that,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842 \textcolor{comment}{//   Do NOT use this class as a std::vector replacement in your own code! Many of the structures used by dear imgui can be safely initialized by a zero-\/memset.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2346 \textcolor{comment}{// We use it to e.g. store collapse state for a tree (Int 0/1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2347 \textcolor{comment}{// This is optimized for efficient lookup (dichotomy into a contiguous buffer) and rare insertion (typically tied to user interactions aka max once a frame)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2348 \textcolor{comment}{// You can use it as custom user storage for temporary values. Declare your own storage if, for example:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2349 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to manipulate the open/close state of a particular sub-\/tree in your interface (tree node uses Int 0/1 to store their state).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2350 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You want to store custom debug data easily without adding or editing structures in your code (probably not efficient, but convenient)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2351 \textcolor{comment}{// Types are NOT stored, so it is up to you to make sure your Key don't collide with different types.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2395 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: Manually clip large list of items.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2396 \textcolor{comment}{// If you have lots evenly spaced items and you have a random access to the list, you can perform coarse}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2397 \textcolor{comment}{// clipping based on visibility to only submit items that are in view.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2398 \textcolor{comment}{// The clipper calculates the range of visible items and advance the cursor to compensate for the non-\/visible items we have skipped.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2399 \textcolor{comment}{// (Dear ImGui already clip items based on their bounds but: it needs to first layout the item to do so, and generally}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2400 \textcolor{comment}{//  fetching/submitting your own data incurs additional cost. Coarse clipping using ImGuiListClipper allows you to easily}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2401 \textcolor{comment}{//  scale using lists with tens of thousands of items without a problem)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2402 \textcolor{comment}{// Usage:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2403 \textcolor{comment}{//   ImGuiListClipper clipper;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2404 \textcolor{comment}{//   clipper.Begin(1000);         // We have 1000 elements, evenly spaced.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2405 \textcolor{comment}{//   while (clipper.Step())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2406 \textcolor{comment}{//       for (int i = clipper.DisplayStart; i < clipper.DisplayEnd; i++)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2407 \textcolor{comment}{//           ImGui::Text("{}line number \%d"{}, i);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2408 \textcolor{comment}{// Generally what happens is:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2409 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper lets you process the first element (DisplayStart = 0, DisplayEnd = 1) regardless of it being visible or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2410 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit that one element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2411 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper can measure the height of the first element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2412 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Clipper calculate the actual range of elements to display based on the current clipping rectangle, position the cursor before the first visible element.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2413 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ User code submit visible elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2414 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The clipper also handles various subtleties related to keyboard/gamepad navigation, wrapping etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2415 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper}{ImGuiListClipper}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2416 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2417     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper_a9d096e06e5633fd77a8a209c00fe454a}{DisplayStart}};       \textcolor{comment}{// First item to display, updated by each call to Step()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2418     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper_aa49e30d04ad8f8b95fbaa62dfbb4ea3e}{DisplayEnd}};         \textcolor{comment}{// End of items to display (exclusive)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2419     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}             \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper_a4e2b4e8efe10615d04ad2aeea467f522}{ItemsCount}};         \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Number of items}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2420     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}           \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper_a19762cb78ff0adccb414027c25678a60}{ItemsHeight}};        \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Height of item after a first step and item submission can calculate it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2421     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float}           \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_list_clipper_affee91b338520cd4bd59b5b680dcb5ae}{StartPosY}};          \textcolor{comment}{// [Internal] Cursor position at the time of Begin() or after table frozen rows are all processed}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2423 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2440 \textcolor{comment}{// Helpers macros to generate 32-\/bit encoded colors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2441 \textcolor{comment}{// User can declare their own format by \#defining the 5 \_SHIFT/\_MASK macros in their imconfig file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2442 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IM\_COL32\_R\_SHIFT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2443 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifdef IMGUI\_USE\_BGRA\_PACKED\_COLOR}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2446 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_B\_SHIFT    0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2447 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_A\_SHIFT    24}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2448 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_A\_MASK     0xFF000000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2449 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2450 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_R\_SHIFT    0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2451 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_G\_SHIFT    8}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2452 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_B\_SHIFT    16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2453 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_A\_SHIFT    24}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2454 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_A\_MASK     0xFF000000}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2455 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2456 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2457 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32(R,G,B,A)    (((ImU32)(A)<<IM\_COL32\_A\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(B)<<IM\_COL32\_B\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(G)<<IM\_COL32\_G\_SHIFT) | ((ImU32)(R)<<IM\_COL32\_R\_SHIFT))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2458 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_WHITE       IM\_COL32(255,255,255,255)  }\textcolor{comment}{// Opaque white = 0xFFFFFFFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2459 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_BLACK       IM\_COL32(0,0,0,255)        }\textcolor{comment}{// Opaque black}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2460 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_COL32\_BLACK\_TRANS IM\_COL32(0,0,0,0)          }\textcolor{comment}{// Transparent black = 0x00000000}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2462 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: ImColor() implicitly converts colors to either ImU32 (packed 4x1 byte) or ImVec4 (4x1 float)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2463 \textcolor{comment}{// Prefer using IM\_COL32() macros if you want a guaranteed compile-\/time ImU32 for usage with ImDrawList API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2464 \textcolor{comment}{// **Avoid storing ImColor! Store either u32 of ImVec4. This is not a full-\/featured color class. MAY OBSOLETE.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2493 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawCallback: Draw callbacks for advanced uses [configurable type: override in imconfig.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2494 \textcolor{comment}{// NB: You most likely do NOT need to use draw callbacks just to create your own widget or customized UI rendering,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2495 \textcolor{comment}{// you can poke into the draw list for that! Draw callback may be useful for example to:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2496 \textcolor{comment}{//  A) Change your GPU render state,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2497 \textcolor{comment}{//  B) render a complex 3D scene inside a UI element without an intermediate texture/render target, etc.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2498 \textcolor{comment}{// The expected behavior from your rendering function is 'if (cmd.UserCallback != NULL) \{ cmd.UserCallback(parent\_list, cmd); \} else \{ RenderTriangles() \}'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2499 \textcolor{comment}{// If you want to override the signature of ImDrawCallback, you can simply use e.g. '\#define ImDrawCallback MyDrawCallback' (in imconfig.h) + update rendering backend accordingly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2500 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef ImDrawCallback}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2504 \textcolor{comment}{// Special Draw callback value to request renderer backend to reset the graphics/render state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2505 \textcolor{comment}{// The renderer backend needs to handle this special value, otherwise it will crash trying to call a function at this address.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2506 \textcolor{comment}{// This is useful for example if you submitted callbacks which you know have altered the render state and you want it to be restored.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2507 \textcolor{comment}{// It is not done by default because they are many perfectly useful way of altering render state for imgui contents (e.g. changing shader/blending settings before an Image call).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2508 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ImDrawCallback\_ResetRenderState     (ImDrawCallback)(-\/1)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2611 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw command list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2612 \textcolor{comment}{// This is the low-\/level list of polygons that ImGui:: functions are filling. At the end of the frame,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2613 \textcolor{comment}{// all command lists are passed to your ImGuiIO::RenderDrawListFn function for rendering.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2614 \textcolor{comment}{// Each dear imgui window contains its own ImDrawList. You can use ImGui::GetWindowDrawList() to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2615 \textcolor{comment}{// access the current window draw list and draw custom primitives.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2616 \textcolor{comment}{// You can interleave normal ImGui:: calls and adding primitives to the current draw list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2617 \textcolor{comment}{// In single viewport mode, top-\/left is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos (generally 0,0), bottom-\/right is == GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos+Size (generally io.DisplaySize).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2618 \textcolor{comment}{// You are totally free to apply whatever transformation matrix to want to the data (depending on the use of the transformation you may want to apply it to ClipRect as well!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2619 \textcolor{comment}{// Important: Primitives are always added to the list and not culled (culling is done at higher-\/level by ImGui:: functions), if you use this API a lot consider coarse culling your drawn objects.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2653     \textcolor{comment}{// Primitives}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2654     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Filled shapes must always use clockwise winding order. The anti-\/aliasing fringe depends on it. Counter-\/clockwise shapes will have "{}inward"{} anti-\/aliasing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2655     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For rectangular primitives, "{}p\_min"{} and "{}p\_max"{} represent the upper-\/left and lower-\/right corners.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2656     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ For circle primitives, use "{}num\_segments == 0"{} to automatically calculate tessellation (preferred).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2657     \textcolor{comment}{//   In older versions (until Dear ImGui 1.77) the AddCircle functions defaulted to num\_segments == 12.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2658     \textcolor{comment}{//   In future versions we will use textures to provide cheaper and higher-\/quality circles.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2659     \textcolor{comment}{//   Use AddNgon() and AddNgonFilled() functions if you need to guaranteed a specific number of sides.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2842     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a80e2e7eb7dc9a76ac5384b9ce6786563a7939beebad9a6cc4c960f2f03b035f60}{ImFontAtlasFlags\_None}}               = 0,}
\DoxyCodeLine{2843     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a80e2e7eb7dc9a76ac5384b9ce6786563a85118b9701f0caf3540e6b542999b999}{ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoPowerOfTwoHeight}} = 1 << 0,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't round the height to next power of two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2844     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a80e2e7eb7dc9a76ac5384b9ce6786563abf2d3e7edd841daaa59af9eb8f2b35fa}{ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors}}     = 1 << 1,   \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build software mouse cursors into the atlas (save a little texture memory)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2845     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_a80e2e7eb7dc9a76ac5384b9ce6786563a69694e359b87dc62b8cad71258b9d976}{ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoBakedLines}}       = 1 << 2    \textcolor{comment}{// Don't build thick line textures into the atlas (save a little texture memory, allow support for point/nearest filtering). The AntiAliasedLinesUseTex features uses them, otherwise they will be rendered using polygons (more expensive for CPU/GPU).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2846 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2847 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2848 \textcolor{comment}{// Load and rasterize multiple TTF/OTF fonts into a same texture. The font atlas will build a single texture holding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2849 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ One or more fonts.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2850 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Custom graphics data needed to render the shapes needed by Dear ImGui.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2851 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Mouse cursor shapes for software cursor rendering (unless setting 'Flags |= ImFontAtlasFlags\_NoMouseCursors' in the font atlas).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2852 \textcolor{comment}{// It is the user-\/code responsibility to setup/build the atlas, then upload the pixel data into a texture accessible by your graphics api.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2853 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Optionally, call any of the AddFont*** functions. If you don't call any, the default font embedded in the code will be loaded for you.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2854 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call GetTexDataAsAlpha8() or GetTexDataAsRGBA32() to build and retrieve pixels data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2855 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Upload the pixels data into a texture within your graphics system (see imgui\_impl\_xxxx.cpp examples)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2856 \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/ Call SetTexID(my\_tex\_id); and pass the pointer/identifier to your texture in a format natural to your graphics API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2857 \textcolor{comment}{//    This value will be passed back to you during rendering to identify the texture. Read FAQ entry about ImTextureID for more details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2858 \textcolor{comment}{// Common pitfalls:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2859 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you pass a 'glyph\_ranges' array to AddFont*** functions, you need to make sure that your array persist up until the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2860 \textcolor{comment}{//   atlas is build (when calling GetTexData*** or Build()). We only copy the pointer, not the data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2861 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important: By default, AddFontFromMemoryTTF() takes ownership of the data. Even though we are not writing to it, we will free the pointer on destruction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2862 \textcolor{comment}{//   You can set font\_cfg-\/>FontDataOwnedByAtlas=false to keep ownership of your data and it won't be freed,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2863 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Even though many functions are suffixed with "{}TTF"{}, OTF data is supported just as well.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2864 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This is an old API and it is currently awkward for those and and various other reasons! We will address them in the future!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2865 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_font_atlas}{ImFontAtlas}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2866 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2880     \textcolor{comment}{// Build atlas, retrieve pixel data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2881     \textcolor{comment}{// User is in charge of copying the pixels into graphics memory (e.g. create a texture with your engine). Then store your texture handle with SetTexID().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2882     \textcolor{comment}{// The pitch is always = Width * BytesPerPixels (1 or 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2883     \textcolor{comment}{// Building in RGBA32 format is provided for convenience and compatibility, but note that unless you manually manipulate or copy color data into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2884     \textcolor{comment}{// the texture (e.g. when using the AddCustomRect*** api), then the RGB pixels emitted will always be white (\string~75\% of memory/bandwidth waste.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2911     \textcolor{comment}{// You can request arbitrary rectangles to be packed into the atlas, for your own purposes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2912     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ After calling Build(), you can query the rectangle position and render your pixels.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2913     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you render colored output, set 'atlas-\/>TexPixelsUseColors = true' as this may help some backends decide of prefered texture format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2914     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can also request your rectangles to be mapped as font glyph (given a font + Unicode point),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2915     \textcolor{comment}{//   so you can render e.g. custom colorful icons and use them as regular glyphs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2916     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Read docs/FONTS.md for more details about using colorful icons.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3034     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_acfbf11da4942c4258ebd9ab9018b2523a2e0134d78faa6cd2efb67bc931b3c5dd}{ImGuiViewportFlags\_TopMost}}                  = 1 << 9,   \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Display on top (for tooltips only).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3035     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_acfbf11da4942c4258ebd9ab9018b2523a67a4dbdf1b3f4cbf417d81a5410bb242}{ImGuiViewportFlags\_Minimized}}                = 1 << 10,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Window is minimized, can skip render. When minimized we tend to avoid using the viewport pos/size for clipping window or testing if they are contained in the viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3036     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_acfbf11da4942c4258ebd9ab9018b2523ae8054f30b31192f16b68aeb22720edce}{ImGuiViewportFlags\_NoAutoMerge}}              = 1 << 11,  \textcolor{comment}{// Platform Window: Avoid merging this window into another host window. This can only be set via ImGuiWindowClass viewport flags override (because we need to now ahead if we are going to create a viewport in the first place!).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3037     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_acfbf11da4942c4258ebd9ab9018b2523a7d2a22003ab5056bcf7ca482cdf99b08}{ImGuiViewportFlags\_CanHostOtherWindows}}      = 1 << 12   \textcolor{comment}{// Main viewport: can host multiple imgui windows (secondary viewports are associated to a single window).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3038 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3040 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Currently represents the Platform Window created by the application which is hosting our Dear ImGui windows.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3041 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ With multi-\/viewport enabled, we extend this concept to have multiple active viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3042 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ In the future we will extend this concept further to also represent Platform Monitor and support a "{}no main platform window"{} operation mode.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3043 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ About Main Area vs Work Area:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3044 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Main Area = entire viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3045 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Work Area = entire viewport minus sections used by main menu bars (for platform windows), or by task bar (for platform monitor).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3046 \textcolor{comment}{//   -\/ Windows are generally trying to stay within the Work Area of their host viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3047 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3062     \textcolor{comment}{// by the same system and you may not need to use all the UserData/Handle fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3063     \textcolor{comment}{// The library never uses those fields, they are merely storage to facilitate backend implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3064     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport_aad757bd8e139bc115edc08dde8c5cad3}{RendererUserData}};       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the renderer (e.g. swap chain, framebuffers etc.). generally set by your Renderer\_CreateWindow function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3065     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*               \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport_a11c62120800d3e7ed83a8c2db23ba2dd}{PlatformUserData}};       \textcolor{comment}{// void* to hold custom data structure for the OS / platform (e.g. windowing info, render context). generally set by your Platform\_CreateWindow function.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3076     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}              \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport_aecb8b050853aae709f64b82319699bf8}{GetCenter}}()\textcolor{keyword}{ const       }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2}{ImVec2}}(Pos.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2_a5802a68560961ed8cb8cc5fb2a244c2d}{x}} + Size.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2_a5802a68560961ed8cb8cc5fb2a244c2d}{x}} * 0.5f, Pos.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2_a1f9d136ca837e147b793b19d25a3a618}{y}} + Size.\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vec2_a1f9d136ca837e147b793b19d25a3a618}{y}} * 0.5f); \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3080 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3081 \textcolor{comment}{// [SECTION] Platform Dependent Interfaces (for e.g. multi-\/viewport support)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3082 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3083 \textcolor{comment}{// [BETA] (Optional) This is completely optional, for advanced users!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3084 \textcolor{comment}{// If you are new to Dear ImGui and trying to integrate it into your engine, you can probably ignore this for now.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3085 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3086 \textcolor{comment}{// This feature allows you to seamlessly drag Dear ImGui windows outside of your application viewport.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3087 \textcolor{comment}{// This is achieved by creating new Platform/OS windows on the fly, and rendering into them.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3088 \textcolor{comment}{// Dear ImGui manages the viewport structures, and the backend create and maintain one Platform/OS window for each of those viewports.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3089 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3090 \textcolor{comment}{// See Glossary https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/wiki/Glossary for details about some of the terminology.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3091 \textcolor{comment}{// See Thread https://github.com/ocornut/imgui/issues/1542 for gifs, news and questions about this evolving feature.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3092 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3093 \textcolor{comment}{// About the coordinates system:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3094 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ When multi-\/viewports are enabled, all Dear ImGui coordinates become absolute coordinates (same as OS coordinates!)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3095 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ So e.g. ImGui::SetNextWindowPos(ImVec2(0,0)) will position a window relative to your primary monitor!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3096 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you want to position windows relative to your main application viewport, use ImGui::GetMainViewport()-\/>Pos as a base position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3097 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3098 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a default backend from the examples/ folder:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3099 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3100 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      The backend initialization will setup all necessary ImGuiPlatformIO's functions and update monitors info every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3101 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3102 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3103 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3104 \textcolor{comment}{// Steps to use multi-\/viewports in your application, when using a custom backend:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3105 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Important:    THIS IS NOT EASY TO DO and comes with many subtleties not described here!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3106 \textcolor{comment}{//                 It's also an experimental feature, so some of the requirements may evolve.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3107 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Consider using default backends if you can. Either way, carefully follow and refer to examples/ backends for details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3108 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Enable feature with 'io.ConfigFlags |= ImGuiConfigFlags\_ViewportsEnable'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3109 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Backend:      Hook ImGuiPlatformIO's Platform\_* and Renderer\_* callbacks (see below).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3110 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Set 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports' and 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags\_PlatformHasViewports'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3111 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update ImGuiPlatformIO's Monitors list every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3112 \textcolor{comment}{//                 Update MousePos every frame, in absolute coordinates.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3113 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  In your main loop, call ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows(), ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() after EndFrame() or Render().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3114 \textcolor{comment}{//                 You may skip calling RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() if its API is not convenient for your needs. Read comments below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3115 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Application:  Fix absolute coordinates used in ImGui::SetWindowPos() or ImGui::SetNextWindowPos() calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3116 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3117 \textcolor{comment}{// About ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault():}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3118 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ This function is a mostly a \_helper\_ for the common-\/most cases, and to facilitate using default backends.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3119 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ You can check its simple source code to understand what it does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3120 \textcolor{comment}{//   It basically iterates secondary viewports and call 4 functions that are setup in ImGuiPlatformIO, if available:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3121 \textcolor{comment}{//     Platform\_RenderWindow(), Renderer\_RenderWindow(), Platform\_SwapBuffers(), Renderer\_SwapBuffers()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3122 \textcolor{comment}{//   Those functions pointers exists only for the benefit of RenderPlatformWindowsDefault().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3123 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you have very specific rendering needs (e.g. flipping multiple swap-\/chain simultaneously, unusual sync/threading issues, etc.),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3124 \textcolor{comment}{//   you may be tempted to ignore RenderPlatformWindowsDefault() and write customized code to perform your renderingg.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3125 \textcolor{comment}{//   You may decide to setup the platform\_io's *RenderWindow and *SwapBuffers pointers and call your functions through those pointers,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3126 \textcolor{comment}{//   or you may decide to never setup those pointers and call your code directly. They are a convenience, not an obligatory interface.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3127 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3128 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3129 \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Access via ImGui::GetPlatformIO()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3130 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_platform_i_o}{ImGuiPlatformIO}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3131 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3132     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3133     \textcolor{comment}{// Input -\/ Backend interface/functions + Monitor List}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3134     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3135 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3136     \textcolor{comment}{// (Optional) Platform functions (e.g. Win32, GLFW, SDL2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3137     \textcolor{comment}{// For reference, the second column shows which function are generally calling the Platform Functions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3138     \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ImGui::NewFrame()                        \string~ beginning of the dear imgui frame: read info from platform/OS windows (latest size/position)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3139     \textcolor{comment}{//   F = ImGui::Begin(), ImGui::EndFrame()        \string~ during the dear imgui frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3140     \textcolor{comment}{//   U = ImGui::UpdatePlatformWindows()           \string~ after the dear imgui frame: create and update all platform/OS windows}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3141     \textcolor{comment}{//   R = ImGui::RenderPlatformWindowsDefault()    \string~ render}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3142     \textcolor{comment}{//   D = ImGui::DestroyPlatformWindows()          \string~ shutdown}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3143     \textcolor{comment}{// The general idea is that NewFrame() we will read the current Platform/OS state, and UpdatePlatformWindows() will write to it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3144     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3145     \textcolor{comment}{// The functions are designed so we can mix and match 2 imgui\_impl\_xxxx files, one for the Platform (\string~window/input handling), one for Renderer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3146     \textcolor{comment}{// Custom engine backends will often provide both Platform and Renderer interfaces and so may not need to use all functions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3147     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform functions are typically called before their Renderer counterpart, apart from Destroy which are called the other way.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3148 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3149     \textcolor{comment}{// Platform function -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ Called by -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3157     \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac668e7cffd9e2e9cfee428b9b2f34fa7}{void}}    (*Platform\_SetWindowFocus)(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}* vp);                  \textcolor{comment}{// N . . . .  // Move window to front and set input focus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3158     bool    (*Platform\_GetWindowFocus)(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_gui_viewport}{ImGuiViewport}}* vp);                  \textcolor{comment}{// . . U . .  //}}
